\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l01071}01071 UndoableCommand::rotate(\textcolor{keywordtype}{double} x, EmbReal y, EmbReal rot)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l01072}01072 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l01073}01073     EmbReal rad = radians(rot);}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l01081}01081     rotv.y = p.x*sinRot + p.y*cosRot;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l01082}01082     rotv.x += x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l01083}01083     rotv.y += y;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03507}03507 \textcolor{comment}{/* Selection box code.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03508}03508 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03509}03509 \textcolor{comment}{ * After normalising the the selection box by changing the ItemSelectionMode,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03510}03510 \textcolor{comment}{ * there are 4 possible selection modes based on the product of the shift key state,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03511}03511 \textcolor{comment}{ * and PICKADD mode.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03512}03512 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03513}03513 \textcolor{comment}{ * SHIFT | PICKADD | ACTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03514}03514 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/|-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/|-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03515}03515 \textcolor{comment}{ * true  | true    | Add current selectbox to the selection.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03516}03516 \textcolor{comment}{ * false | true    | Remove current selectbox from the selection.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03517}03517 \textcolor{comment}{ * true  | false   | If the selectbox is empty, clear the selection,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03518}03518 \textcolor{comment}{ *       |         | otherwise toggle the state of the contents of the selectbox.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03519}03519 \textcolor{comment}{ * false | false   | Replace the selection with the selectbox contents.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03520}03520 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03764}03764             EmbReal cosRot = cos(rad);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03765}03765             EmbReal sinRot = sin(rad);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03766}03766             EmbVector p, rotv;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03767}03767             p.x = -\/x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03768}03768             p.y = -\/y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03769}03769             rotv.x = p.x*cosRot -\/ p.y*sinRot;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03770}03770             rotv.y = p.x*sinRot + p.y*cosRot;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03771}03771             rotv.x += x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l03772}03772             rotv.y += y;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l06633}06633 \textcolor{comment}{/* For each Command in command\_data, for each alias set up a map from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l06634}06634 \textcolor{comment}{ * alias to the Command. Then for a given context the call doesn't have to loop?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l06635}06635 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l06636}06636 \textcolor{comment}{ * NOTE:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l06637}06637 \textcolor{comment}{ * Every action must have a unique constant identifier of the form "{}ACTION\_*"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l06638}06638 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l06639}06639 \textcolor{comment}{ * If every function was called main(), then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l06640}06640 \textcolor{comment}{ * the ScriptArgs would only call the last script evaluated (which happens to be main() in another script).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l06641}06641 \textcolor{comment}{ * Thus, by adding the cmdName before main(), it becomes line\_main(), circle\_main(), etc...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l06642}06642 \textcolor{comment}{ * Do not change this code unless you really know what you are doing. I mean it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l06643}06643 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l06644}06644 \textcolor{comment}{ * Position currently comes from the order of the command\_data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l06645}06645 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l06646}06646 \textcolor{comment}{ * TODO:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l06647}06647 \textcolor{comment}{ * Set What's This Context Help to statusTip for now so there is some infos there.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l06648}06648 \textcolor{comment}{ * Make custom whats this context help popup with more descriptive help than just}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l06649}06649 \textcolor{comment}{ * the status bar/tip one liner(short but not real long) with a hyperlink in the custom popup}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l06650}06650 \textcolor{comment}{ * at the bottom to open full help file description. Ex: like wxPython AGW's SuperToolTip.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l06651}06651 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{commands_8cpp_source_l06652}06652 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}}
